       beforeAll(function () {\n            fuzzyScore = window.CommandPaletteManager._fuzzyScore;\n        });\n\n        it('returns 1 for exact match', function () {\n       });\n\n        it('\"ktchn\" → \"Kitchen\" scores >= 0.3 (subsequence)', function () {\n            expect(fuzzyScore('ktchn', 'Kitchen')).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(0.3);\n        });\n\n \"Kitchen\" scores < 0.3 (excluded)', function () {\n            expect(fuzzyScore('xyz', 'Kitchen')).toBeLessThan(0.3);\n        });\n\n        it('\"living room\" → \"Living Room\" scores >= 0.8        var expectedMax = after.getTime()  - 30 * 60 * 1000;\n            expect(d.getTime()).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(expectedMin - 1000);\n prev[k - 1]\n46\t                    : 1 + Math.min(prev[k], curr[k - 1], prev[k - 1]);\n47\t            }\n48\t            var tmp = prev; prev = curr; curr = tmp;\n49\t        }\n50\t        return prev[n];\n51\t    }\n52\t\n53\t    // =========================================================\n54\t    // Fuzzy scorer  [0, 1]\n55\t    // =========================================================\n56\t    /**\n57\t     * Returns a score in [0, 1] indicating how well `needle` matches `haystack`.\n58\t     * Scores below 0.3 are considered non-matches and are excluded from results.\n59\t     *\n60\t     * Matching strategy (in priority order):\n61\t     *   1. Exact prefix of full haystack              → 0.90–1.00\n62\t     *   2. Exact substring of full haystack           → 0.80\n63\t     *   3. Word-level matching (prefix / typo / subseq per word)\n64\t     *   4. Character subsequence across full string   → 0.30–0.40\n65\t     */\n66\t    function fuzzyScore(needle, haystack) {\n67\t        if (!needle) return 1;\n68\t        needle   = needle.toLowerCase().trim();\n69\t        haystack = haystack.toLowerCase().trim();\n70\t        if (!needle) return 1;\n71\t        if (needle === haystack) return 1;\n72\t\n73\t        // 1. Full prefix\n74\t        if (haystack.startsWith(needle)) {\n75\t            return 0.90 + 0.10 * (needle.length / haystack.length);\n76\t        }\n77\t\n78\t        // 2. Exact substring\n79\t        if (haystack.includes(needle)) {\n80\t            return 0.80;\n81\t        }\n82\t\n83\t        // 3. });\n86\t\n87\t        if (needleWords.length > 0) {\n88\t            var allMatch   = true;\n89\t            var totalScore = 0;\n90\t\n91\t            for (var ni = 0; ni < needleWords.length; ni++) {\n92\t                var nw = needleWords[ni];\n93\t                var bestWord = 0;\n94\t\n95\t                for (var hi = 0; ci < hw.length && si < nw.length; ci++) {\n114\t                                if (nw[si] === hw[ci]) si++;\n115\t                            }\n116\t                            if (si === nw.length) ws = 0.50;\n117\t                        }\n118\t                    } else if (nw.length <= 2) {\n119\t                        // Short needle: prefix or subsequence within each haystack word\n120\t                        if (hw.startsWith(nw)) {\n121\t                            ws = 0.75;\n122\t                        } else {\n123\t                            var si2 = 0;\n124\t                            for (var ci2 = 0; ci2 < hw.length && si2 < nw.length; ci2++) {\n125\t                                if (nw[si2] === hw[ci2]) si2++;\n126\t                            }\n127\t                            if (si2 === nw.length) ws = 0.50;\n128\t                        }\n129\t                    }\n130\t\n131\t                    if (ws > bestWord) bestWord = ws;\n132\t                }\n133\t\n134\t                if (bestWord === 0) {\n135\t                    allMatch = false;\n136\t                    break;\n137\t                }\n138\t                totalScore += bestWord;\n139\t            }\n140\t\n141\t            if (allMatch) {\n142\t                return 0.40 + (totalScore / needleWords.length) * 0.30;\n143\t            }\n144\t        }\n145\t\n146\t        // 4. Character subsequence across full string\n147\t        var si3 = 0;\n148\t        for (var ci3 = 0; ci3 < haystack.length && si3 < needle.length; ci3++) {\n149\t            if (needle[si3] === haystack[ci3]) si3++;\n150\t        }\n151\t        if (si3 === needle.length) {\n152\t            return 0.30 + 0.10 * (needle.length / haystack.length);\n153\t        }\n154\t\n155\t        return 0;\n156\t    }\n157\t\n158\t    // =========================================================\n159\t    // Time expression parser\n160\t    // =========================================================\n161\t    /**\n162\t     * Parse a \"@...\" time expression.\n163\t     * @param {string} query - full query string starting with \"@\"\n164\t     * @returns {Date|null}\n165\t     */\n166\t    function parseTimeExpression(query) {\n167\t        var s = query.replace(/^@/, '').trim();\n168\t        if (!s) return null;\n169\t        var now = new Date();\n170\t\n171\t        // @-30min  @-2h\n172\t        var rel = s.match(/^-(\\d+)(min|h)$/i);\n173\t        if (rel) {\n174\t            var amount = parseInt(rel[1], 10);\n175\t r2.setHours(parseInt(m24[1], 10), parseInt(m24[2], 10), 0, 0);\n238\t            return r2;\n239\t        }\n240\t        return null;\n241\t    }\n242\t\n243\t    // (localStorage)\n745\t    // =========================================================\n746\t    function loadHistory() {\n747\t        try {\n748\t            return }\n761\t\n762\t    function addToHistory(item) {\n763\t        // Exclude time navigation entries\n764\t        if (item.category === 'time') return;\n765\t        var hist = saveHistory(hist);\n768\t    }\n769\t\n770\t    // =========================================================\n771\t    // Entity data source\n772\t    // data;\n795\t    }\n796\t\n797\t    // =========================================================\n798\t    // Search\n799\t    // =========================================================\n800\t    /**\n801\t     * Search all categories with the given query.\n802\t     * @param {string} query\n803\t     * @returns {Array} sorted result items\n804\t     */\n805\t    function search(query) {\n806\t        var results = [];\n807\t        var q = query.trim();\n808\t\n809\t        // Empty query: show recent history\n810\t        if (!q) {\n811\t            var hist = loadHistory();\n812\t            return hist.slice(0, MAX_RECENT).map(function (h) {\n813\t                return {\n814\t                    id:       h.id,\n815\t                    label:    h.label,\n816\t                    category: 'recent',\n817\t                    icon:     h.icon || '🕐',\n818\t                    secondary: 'Recent',\n819\t                    score:    1,\n820\t                    action:   findCommandAction(h.id)\n821\t                };\n822\t            });\n823\t        }\n824\t\n825\t        // Time navigation\n826\t        if (q.startsWith('@')) {\n827\t            var dt = parseTimeExpression(q);\n828\t            if (dt) {\n829\t                var label = 'Jump to ' + dt.toLocaleString();\n830\t                results.push({\n831\t                          window.SpaxelReplay.seekTo(dt.getTime());\n840\t                        }\n841\t                    }\n842\t                });\n843\t            }\n844\t            return results;\n845\t        }\n846\t\n847\t        var entities = getEntityData();\n848\t\n849\t        // Commands\n850\t        COMMANDS.forEach(function (cmd) {\n851\t            var s = Math.max(\n852\t                fuzzyScore(q, cmd.label),\n853\t                fuzzyScore(q, cmd.group || '')\n854\t            );\n855\t            if (s >= 0.3) {\n856\t                results.push({\n857\t                    id:       cmd.id,\n858\t                    label:    cmd.label,\n859\t                    category: 'command',\n860\t                    icon:     cmd.icon,\n861\t                    secondary: cmd.group || '',\n862\t                    hint:     cmd.hint || '',\n863\t                    score:    s,\n864\t                    action:   cmd.action\n865\t                });\n866\t            }\n867\t        });\n868\t\n869\t        // People\n870\t        entities.people.forEach(function (p) {\n871\t            var name = p.name || p.label || p.addr || '';\n872\t            var s = fuzzyScore(q, name);\n873\t            if (s >= 0.3) {\n874\t                results.push({\n875\t                    id:       'person:' + name,\n876\t                    label:    name,\n877\t                    category: 'person',\n878\t                    icon:     '👤',\n879\t                    secondary: p.zone || '',\n880\t                    score:    s,\n881\t                    action: function () {\n882\t                        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.flyToPerson) window.Viz3D.flyToPerson(name);\n883\t                    }\n884\t                });\n885\t            }\n886\t        });\n887\t\n888\t        // Zones\n889\t        entities.zones.forEach(function (z) {\n890\t            var name = z.name || '';\n891\t            var s = fuzzyScore(q, name);\n892\t            if (s >= 0.3) {\n893\t                var count = z.count != null ? z.count : (z.occupancy || 0);\n894\t                results.push({\n895\t                    id:       'zone:' + name,\n896\t                    label:    name,\n897\t                    category: 'zone',\n898\t                    icon:     '📍',\n899\t                    secondary: count + ' people currently',\n900\t                    score:    s,\n901\t                    action: function () {\n902\t                        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.flyToZone) window.Viz3D.flyToZone(name);\n903\t                    }\n904\t                });\n905\t            }\n906\t        });\n907\t\n908\t        // Nodes\n909\t        entities.nodes.forEach(function (n) {\n910\t            var label = n.name || n.mac || '';\n911\t            var s = Math.max(\n912\t                fuzzyScore(q, label),\n913\t                n.mac ? fuzzyScore(q, n.mac) : 0\n914\t            );\n915\t            if (s >= 0.3) {\n916\t                results.push({\n917\t                    id:       'node:' + (n.mac || label),\n918\t                    label:    label,\n919\t                    category: 'node',\n920\t                    icon:     '📡',\n921\t                    secondary: n.status || '',\n922\t                    score:    s,\n923\t                    action: function () {\n924\t                        if (window.Viz3D && window.Viz3D.flyToNode && n.mac) window.Viz3D.flyToNode(n.mac);\n925\t                    }\n926\t                });\n927\t            }\n928\t        });\n929\t\n930\t        // Recent events (last 20)\n931\t        entities.events.forEach(function (evt) {\n932\t            var title = evt.title || evt.type || '';\n933\t            var s = fuzzyScore(q, title);\n934\t            if (s >= 0.3) {\n935\t                results.push({\n936\t                    id:       'event:' + (evt.id ||                score:    s,\n942\t                    action: function () {\n943\t                        if (window.SpaxelTimeline && window.SpaxelTimeline.openEvent) {\n944\t                            window.SpaxelTimeline.openEvent(evt.id);\n945\t                        }\n946\t                    }\n947\t                });\n948\t            }\n949\t        });\n950\t\n951\t        // Sort: commands first (if query starts with \"/\"), then by category priority, then score desc\n952\t        results.sort(function (a, b) {\n953\t            var pa = CAT_PRIORITY[a.category] != null ? CAT_PRIORITY[a.category] : 99;\n954\t            var pb = CAT_PRIORITY[b.category] != null ? CAT_PRIORITY[b.category] : 99;\n955\t            if (pa !== pb) return pa - pb;\n956\t            return b.score - a.score;\n957\t        });\n958\t\n959\t        return results.slice(0, MAX_RESULTS);\n960\t    }\n961\t\n962\t    function findCommandAction(id) {\n963\t        for (var i = 0; i < COMMANDS.length; i++) {\n964\t            if (COMMANDS[i].id === id) return COMMANDS[i].action;\n965\t        }\n966\t        return function () {};\n967\t    }\n968\t\n969\t    // =========================================================\n970\t    // Mode detection\n971\t    // =========================================================\n972\t    function isPaletteAvailable() {\n973\t        if (document.body.classList.contains('ambient-mode')) return false;\n974\t        if (window.currentMode === 'ambient') return false;\n975\t        return true;\n976\t    }\n977\t\n978\t    // =========================================================\n979\t    // DOM {\n1010\t        var list = document.getElementById('cp-listbox');\n1011\t        if (!list) return;\n1012\t\n1013\t        if (!items.length) {\n1014\t            list.innerHTML = '<li            .replace(/</g, '&lt;')\n1063\t            .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')\n1064\t            .replace(/\"/g, '&quot;');\n1065\t    }\n1066\t\n1067\t    // : []);\n1087\t            Manager._entityCache.events = arr.slice(0, 20).map(function (e) {\n1088\t                return { id: e.id, title: e.type || '', zone: e.zone || '', ts: e.timestamp_ms * Spaxel Dashboard — Command Palette (Component 34)\n *\n * Ctrl+K / Cmd+K: universal keyboard-driven command interface.\n * Fuzzy search across zones, people, nodes, events, and commands.\n * Time navigation via \"@\" prefix.\n *\n * Exposes: window.CommandPaletteManager\n */\n\n(function () {\n    'use strict';\n\n    // =========================================================\n    // Constants\n    // =========================================================\n    var STORAGE_KEY = 'spaxel_palette_history';\n    var MAX_RECENT  = 5;\n    var MAX_RESULTS = 8;\n\n    // Category priority (lower = higher in results)\n    var CAT_PRIORITY = {\n        command:   0,\n        time:      1,\n        person:    2,\n        zone:      3,\n        node:      4,\n        event:     5,\n        recent:   -1   // shown only on empty query\n    };\n\n    // =========================================================\n    // Levenshtein distance (compact)\n    // =========================================================\n    function levenshteinDist(a, b) {\n        var m = a.length, n = b.length;\n        if (!m) return n;\n        if (!n) return m;\n        var prev = [], curr = [];\n        for (var j = 0; j <= n; j++) prev[j] = j;\n        for (var i = 1; i <= m; i++) {\n            curr[0] = i;\n            for (var k = 1; k <= n; k++) {\n                curr[k] = a[i - 1] === b[k - 1]\n                    ? prev[k - 1]\n                    : 1 + Math.min(prev[k], curr[k - 1], prev[k - 1]);\n            }\n            var tmp = prev; prev = curr; curr = tmp;\n        }\n        return prev[n];\n    }\n\n    // =========================================================\n    // Fuzzy scorer  [0, 1]\n    // =========================================================\n    /**\n     * Returns a score in [0, 1] indicating how well `needle` matches `haystack`.\n     * Scores below 0.3 are considered non-matches and are excluded from results.\n     *\n     * Matching strategy (in priority order):\n     *   1. Exact prefix of full haystack              → 0.90–1.00\n     *   2. Exact substring of full haystack           → 0.80\n     *   3. Word-level matching (prefix / typo / subseq per word)\n     *   4. Character subsequence across full string   → 0.30–0.40\n     */\n    function fuzzyScore(needle, haystack) {\n        if (!needle) return 1;\n        needle   = needle.toLowerCase().trim();\n        haystack = haystack.toLowerCase().trim();\n        if (!needle) return 1;\n        if (needle === haystack) return 1;\n\n        // 1. Full prefix\n        if (haystack.startsWith(needle)) {\n            return 0.90 + 0.10 * (needle.length / haystack.length);\n        }\n\n        // 2. Exact substring\n        if (haystack.includes(needle)) {\n            return 0.80;\n        }\n\n        // 3. Word-level matching\n        var needleWords   = needle.split(/\\s+/).filter(function (w) { return w.length > 0; });\n        var haystackWords = haystack.split(/\\s+/).filter(function (w) { return w.length > 0; });\n\n        if (needleWords.length > 0) {\n            var allMatch   = true;\n            var totalScore = 0;\n\n            for (var ni = 0; ni < needleWords.length; ni++) {\n                var nw = needleWords[ni];\n                var bestWord = 0;\n\n                for (var hi = 0; hi < haystackWords.length; hi++) {\n                    var hw = haystackWords[hi];\n                    var ws = 0;\n\n                    if (hw.startsWith(nw)) {\n                        ws = 0.90;\n                    } else if (hw.includes(nw)) {\n                        ws = 0.75;\n                    } else if (nw.length > 2 && hw.length > 2) {\n                        var dist = levenshteinDist(nw, hw);\n                        if (dist === 1) {\n                            ws = 0.70;\n                        } else if (dist === 2 && nw.length > 4) {\n                            ws = 0.50;\n                        }\n                        // Per-word subsequence (e.g. \"rm\" in \"room\")\n                        if (ws === 0) {\n                            var si = 0;\n                            for (var ci = 0; ci < hw.length && si < nw.length; ci++) {\n                                if (nw[si] === hw[ci]) si++;\n                            }\n                            if (si === nw.length) ws = 0.50;\n                        }\n                    } else if (nw.length <= 2) {\n                        // Short needle: prefix or subsequence within each haystack word\n                        if (hw.startsWith(nw)) {\n                            ws = 0.75;\n                        } else {\n                            var si2 = 0;\n                            for (var ci2 = 0; ci2 < hw.length && si2 < nw.length; ci2++) {\n                                if (nw[si2] === hw[ci2]) si2++;\n                            }\n                            if (si2 === nw.length) ws = 0.50;\n                        }\n                    }\n\n                    if (ws > bestWord) bestWord = ws;\n                }\n\n                if (bestWord === 0) {\n                    allMatch = false;\n                    break;\n                }\n                totalScore += bestWord;\n            }\n\n            if (allMatch) {\n                return 0.40 + (totalScore / needleWords.length) * 0.30;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // 4. Character subsequence across full string\n        var si3 = 0;\n        for (var ci3 = 0; ci3 < haystack.length && si3 < needle.length; ci3++) {\n            if (needle[si3] === haystack[ci3]) si3++;\n        }\n        if (si3 === needle.length) {\n            return 0.30 + 0.10 * (needle.length / haystack.length);\n        }\n\n        return 0;\n    }\n\n    // =========================================================\n    // Time expression parser\n    // =========================================================\n    /**\n     * Parse a \"@...\" time expression.\n     * @param {string} query - full query string starting with \"@\"\n     * @returns {Date|null}\n     */\n    function parseTimeExpression(query) {\n        var s = query.replace(/^@/, '').trim();\n        if (!s) return null;\n        var now = new Date();\n\n        // @-30min  @-2h\n        var rel = s.match(/^-(\\d+)(min|h)$/i);\n        if (rel) {\n            var amount = parseInt(rel[1], 10);\n            var unit   = rel[2].toLowerCase();\n            var d = new Date(now);\n            if (unit === 'min') d.setMinutes(d.getMinutes() - amount);\n            else                d.setHours(d.getHours() - amount);\n            return d;\n        }\n\n        // @2026-03-27 14:23\n        var abs = s.match(/^(\\d{4}-\\d{2}-\\d{2})\\s+(\\d{1,2}:\\d{2})$/);\n        if (abs) {\n            var dt = new Date(abs[1] + 'T' + abs[2] + ':00');\n            if (!isNaN(dt.getTime())) return dt;\n        }\n\n        // @this morning → today at 06:00\n        if (/^this\\s+morning$/i.test(s)) {\n            var morning = new Date(now);\n            morning.setHours(6, 0, 0, 0);\n            return morning;\n        }\n\n        // @last night → yesterday at 22:00\n        if (/^last\\s+night$/i.test(s)) {\n            var lastNight = new Date(now);\n            lastNight.setHours(22, 0, 0, 0);\n            if (now.getHours() < 6) {\n                // Before 6am — \"last night\" was yesterday\n            } else {\n                lastNight.setDate(lastNight.getDate() - 1);\n            }\n            return lastNight;\n        }\n\n        // @yesterday ...\n        var yest = s.match(/^yesterday\\s+(.+)$/i);\n        if (yest) {\n            var base = new Date(now);\n            base.setDate(base.getDate() - 1);\n            return parseTimeOfDay(yest[1], base);\n        }\n\n        // @3am  @3:15pm  @14:23\n        return parseTimeOfDay(s, new Date(now));\n    }\n\n    function parseTimeOfDay(s, baseDate) {\n        // 12-hour: 3am, 3:15am, 11:30pm\n        var m12 = s.match(/^(\\d{1,2})(?::(\\d{2}))?\\s*(am|pm)$/i);\n        if (m12) {\n            var h = parseInt(m12[1], 10);\n            var min = m12[2] ? parseInt(m12[2], 10) : 0;\n            var ampm = m12[3].toLowerCase();\n            if (ampm === 'pm' && h !== 12) h += 12;\n            if (ampm === 'am' && h === 12) h = 0;\n            var r = new Date(baseDate);\n            r.setHours(h, min, 0, 0);\n            return r;\n        }\n        // 24-hour: 14:23\n        var m24 = s.match(/^(\\d{1,2}):(\\d{2})$/);\n        if (m24) {\n            var r2 = new Date(baseDate);\n            r2.setHours(parseInt(m24[1], 10), parseInt(m24[2], 10), 0, 0);\n            return r2;\n        }\n        return null;\n    }\n\n    // tracking:**\n422\t- Records predictions when made (personID, currentZone, predictedZone, confidence, horizon)\n423\t- Evaluates pending predictions when target time is reached\n424\t- Compares predicted zone vs actual zone\n425\t- Computes rolling 7-day accuracy percentage\n426\t- Reports \"meets_target\" when accuracy ≥ 75% and min predictions threshold met\n427\t\n428\t**Model learning:**\n429\t- Observations recorded every 5 minutes per person/zone\n430\t- EMA update: `p_new = p_old + α × (obs - p_old)` where α = 0.03\n431\t- Cold start: 7 days of data required for model readiness\n432\t- Slot ready when sample_count ≥ 3\n433\t- Automatic recomputation triggered on zone transitions\n434\t\n435\t**Files Complex CSI computation: int8 I/Q → float64 complex → amplitude/phase\n  - RSSI normalization (AGC compensation): `norm = 10^((rssi_ref - rssi)/20)`\n  - Spatial phase unwrapping: correct 2π jumps between adjacent subcarriers\n  - Linear regression (OLS): fit `phase = a*k + b` over data subcarriers\n  - STO/CFO removal: residual phase = unwrapped - (slope × k + intercept)\n  - HT20 subcarrier map: 64 total, 46 data (excluding null, guard, pilot)\n\n- **Baseline system (`signal/baseline.go`):**\n  - EMA baseline per link per subcarrier: `baseline = α×amplitude + (1-α)×baseline`\n  - α = dt / (τ + dt) ≈ 0.0033 for dt=0.1s, τ=30s\n  - Motion-gated updates: only update when smoothDeltaRMS < 0.05\n  - Confidence scoring: 0.3 for stale baselines (>7 days), asymptotically → 1.0\n  - Snapshot/restore for SQLite persistence\n  - BaselineManager for multi-link coordination\n\n- **Motion detection (`signal/features.go`):**\n  - NBVI (Normalized Bandwidth Variance Index): `Var(amp) / Mean(amp)²`\n  - Welford's online algorithm for numerically stable variance\n  - Top-16 subcarrier selection by NBVI score\n  - deltaRMS: `sqrt(mean((amp - baseline)²))` over selected subcarriers\n  - Exponential smoothing: `smooth = 0.3×raw + 0.7×prev`\n  - Motion threshold: smoothDeltaRMS > 0.02\n\n- **Link processor (`signal/processor.go`):**\n  - LinkProcessor: ties together phase sanitization, baseline, motion detection\n  - ProcessorManager: manages per-link processors with thread-safe access\n  - GetAllMotionStates(): returns motion state for all links\n  - GetAllBaselines()/RestoreBaseline(): for SQLite persistence\n\n**Constants used (from plan):**\n- RSSIRefdBm = -30.0\n- DefaultMotionThreshold = 0.05\n- DefaultDeltaRMSThreshold = 0.02\n- NBVITopCount = 16\n- NBVIMinThreshold = 0.001\n- DeltaRMSSmoothingAlpha = 0.3\n\n**Tests:** 37 tests covering phase sanitization, baseline, NBVI, motion detection. All pass.\n\n**Files created:**\n```\nmothership/internal/signal/\n├── phase.go          — Phase sanitization algorithms\n├── phase_test.go     — 15 tests for phase processing\n├── baseline.go       — EMA baseline management\n├── baseline_test.go  — 9 tests for baseline\n├── features.go       — NBVI selection, deltaRMS, motion detection\n├── features_test.go  — 13 tests for features\n└── processor.go      — LinkProcessor, ProcessorManager\n```\n\n**Remaining for Phase 2:**\n- Dashboard presence indicator\n- CSI recording buffer\n- Adaptive sensing rate\n\n#### Iteration 4 — 2026-03-26\n\n**Completed:** Docker packaging\n\nImplemented container deployment with:\n\n- **Dockerfile:** Multi-stage build for minimal production image\n  - AccuracyTracker with rolling 7-day window\n\n**Phase 7 Status:** COMPLETE\n\n## Phase 8 — Analysis & Developer Tools\n\nGoal: Deep debugging, system tuning, and detection explainability.\n\n### /api/events` with cursor-based pagination, filters (type/zone/person/time), and FTS5 search\n- Frontend: `sidebar-timeline.js` — virtualized list, tap-to-time-travel, inline feedback buttons\n\n**Detection explainability (`internal/explainability/`):**\n- `Handler` maintains per-blob explanation data updated by the fusion engine\n- Per-link contribution table: deltaRMS, Fresnel zone number, learned weight, contribution amount\n- BLE match details: per-node RSSI, triangulation position, confidence\n- Fresnel zone ellipsoid geometry for 3D visualization\n- Frontend: (recv_time_ms + raw CSI binary)\n- `Worker` manages replay sessions: play/pause/seek/speed control\n- Parameter tuning: `PATCH /api/replay/params` re-runs pipeline on buffered data at max speed\n- \"Apply to Live\" copies tuned params to the running pipeline\n- Dashboard: timeline scrubber integrated with activity timeline events\n\n**Pre-deployment simulator (`internal/simulator/`):**\n- `Space` defines room geometry with wall segments and material properties\n- `NodeSet` manages virtual TX/RX node placement\n- `WalkerSet` simulates random-walk or path-following persons\n- Two-ray propagation model with path loss + wall penetration + first-order reflections\n- GDOP computation per cell using Fisher information matrix\n- REST API at `/api/simulator/*` for space/node/walker management and GDOP computation\n\n**CSI simulator CLI (`cmd/sim/`):**\n- Connects to mothership as virtual nodes, sends synthetic CSI binary frames\n- Walker random-walk model with Gaussian velocity updates, wall reflection\n- Amplitude/phase generated from propagation model with Gaussian noise injection\n- Optional BLE advertisement simulation (`--ble` flag)\n- Verified authentication (exits non-zero on `{type:\"reject\"}`)\n- Integration test support: polls `GET /api/blobs` for blob count assertions\n\n**Fresnel zone debug overlay (`dashboard/js/fresnel.js`):**\n- Toggle-able wireframe ellipsoids between active TX/RX link pairs\n- Ellipsoid geometry computed from TX/RX positions and Fresnel zone number\n- Color-coded by zone number (zone 1 = bright, outer zones = dimmer)\n- Toolbar button integration with existing layers panel\n\n**Files created/modified:**\n```\nmothership/internal/timeline/       — timeline.go, timeline_test.go, handler.go, per-user default stored in `localStorage`\n\n**Ambient dashboard (`dashboard/ambient.html`, `dashboard/js/ambient.js`):**\n- Served at `/ambient` — separate lightweight route for wall-mounted tablets\n- Canvas 2D renderer: colored circles for people, zone labels, soft glow effects\n- Time-of-day palette: morning (cool), day (neutral), evening (amber), night (very dim)\n- Auto-dim when house empty for 30+ min; gentle fade-in on person detection\n- Alert mode: pulsing red border + large text + action buttons on fall/security events\n- Morning briefing integration: briefing text shown on first detection, fades after 30 s\n- Reconnect backoff handles WebSocket drops gracefully\n\n**Spatial quick actions (`dashboard/js/quick-actions.js`):**\n- Three.js Raycaster determines target under cursor (person/node/zone/portal/trigger/empty)\n- Context menu component renders appropriate options per target type\n- Per-blob: \"Who is this?\", \"Why?\", \"Follow\" camera, \"Create automation\", \"Mark incorrect\"\n- Per-node: \"Diagnostics\", \"Blink LED\", \"Reposition\", \"Update firmware\", \"Show links\"\n- Per-empty: \"What happened here?\", \"Add trigger zone\", \"Add virtual node\", \"Coverage quality\"\n- Per-zone: \"Zone history\", \"Edit zone\", \"Create automation\", \"Crowd flow\"\n- \"Follow\" mode: camera smoothly tracks person, auto-orbiting to keep them centered\n\n**Command palette (`dashboard/js/command-palette.js`):**\n- Ctrl+K (Cmd+K on Mac) opens universal search and command interface\n- Fuzzy matching across zones, persons, nodes, settings, help topics, events\n- Navigate time: \"last night 2am\", \"yesterday kitchen\", \"this morning\"\n- Execute commands: \"update all nodes\", \"re-baseline kitchen\", \"arm security\"\n- Help: \"help fall detection\", \"why false positive\", \"troubleshoot kitchen\"\n- Recently used commands surface first; expert mode only\n\n**Morning briefing (`internal/briefing/`, `dashboard/js/briefing.js`):**\n- `Generator` assembles briefing in priority order from sleep, events, anomalies, system health\n- Priority blocks: critical alerts → sleep summary → who is home → overnight anomalies → system health → predictions → learning progress\n- Degenerate case: \"All quiet last night. All systems healthy.\"\n- Stored in `briefings` SQLite table (one per day per person)\n- REST API: `GET /api/briefing`, `GET /api/briefing/current`\n- Dashboard: card overlay on first open, dismissible, slides away after 10 s\n\n**Guided troubleshooting (`internal/guidedtroubleshoot/`, `dashboard/js/troubleshoot.js`):**\n- Trigger conditions: detection quality drops, repeated setting changes, node offline >2 h\n- Repeated-edit detection: per-key counter in memory; hint delivered in `GET /api/settings` response as `\"repeated_edit_hint\": true`\n- Proactive diagnostic flow: check connectivity → show link health → suggest repositioning → offer re-baseline\n- First-time feature tooltips shown once, dismissed on click, stored in `localStorage`\n- Post-feedback explanations in timeline after incorrect/missed detection feedback\n\n**Mobile-responsive expert mode (`dashboard/js/mobile.js` + CSS):**\n- Touch orbit (one finger), pan (two fingers), pinch-zoom (two fingers)\n- FXAA anti-aliasing replaces MSAA on mobile (better performance on low-power GPUs)\n- Hamburger menu for toolbar panels on small screens\n- Viewport meta tag with `viewport-fit=cover` for notch-aware layout\n- CSS Grid layout collapses gracefully on narrow viewports\n\n**Fleet status page (`dashboard/fleet.html`, `dashboard/js/fleet-page.js`):**\n- Full table with sortable columns: Name, MAC, Role, Position (fly-to), Firmware, RSSI, Status, Uptime, Actions\n- OTA progress bar per node during updates (PENDING → DOWNLOADING → REBOOTING → VERIFIED / FAILED)\n- Bulk actions: Update All (rolling OTA), Re-baseline All, Export Config, Import Config\n- Camera fly-to: clicking position coordinates in table jumps 3D camera to that node\n- Responsive layout works on both desktop and tablet\n\n**Files created/modified:**\n```\ndashboard/simple.html               — Simple mode page\ndashboard/ambient.html              — Ambient dashboard page\ndashboard/fleet.html                —
